              <div class="replyContainer style-scope gr-change-view">
                  <gr-button id="replyBtn" class="reply style-scope gr-change-view x-scope gr-button-8" primary="" role="button" tabindex="0" hidden="true"><paper-button tabindex="-1" class="style-scope gr-button x-scope paper-button-0" role="button" animated="" aria-disabled="false" elevation="1" raised="" style="">Reply<i class="downArrow style-scope gr-button"></i></paper-button></gr-button>
              </div>
              <div id="commitMessage" class="commitMessage  style-scope gr-change-view">
                <gr-editable-content id="commitMessageEditor" remove-zero-width-space="" class="style-scope gr-change-view x-scope gr-editable-content-0">
    
    <div class="style-scope gr-editable-content">
      
                  <gr-linked-text pre="" remove-zero-width-space="" class="style-scope gr-change-view x-scope gr-linked-text-0">
    
    <span id="output" class="style-scope gr-linked-text">Fix CrashDumpManager reporting

file_size was never being set, so OOMs were being reported for normal
foreground crashes.

This CL removes file_size in favor of just using |status| to identify
empty crash dumps.

Unfortunately, this would have been caught if a TODO to beef up the
testing infrastructure had been done. This CL implements those changes
required to regression test this bug.

Bug: <a href="https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=846165" class="style-scope gr-linked-text" target="_blank" rel="noopener">846165</a>
Change-Id: <a href="/q/Ibf272588af4029887792bffec509e0fbdfe9f63b" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="style-scope gr-linked-text">Ibf272588af4029887792bffec509e0fbdfe9f63b</a>
Reviewed-on: <a href="https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/1070794" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="style-scope gr-linked-text">https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/1070794</a>
Reviewed-by: Siddhartha S &lt;<a href="mailto:ssid@chromium.org" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="style-scope gr-linked-text">ssid@chromium.org</a>&gt;
Reviewed-by: Robert Sesek &lt;<a href="mailto:rsesek@chromium.org" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="style-scope gr-linked-text">rsesek@chromium.org</a>&gt;
Reviewed-by: Ryan Sturm &lt;<a href="mailto:ryansturm@chromium.org" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="style-scope gr-linked-text">ryansturm@chromium.org</a>&gt;
Commit-Queue: Charlie Harrison &lt;<a href="mailto:csharrison@chromium.org" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="style-scope gr-linked-text">csharrison@chromium.org</a>&gt;
Cr-Commit-Position: refs/heads/master@{#562694}</span>
  </gr-linked-text>
